 aisa karne se aapke container lambey samay tak aapke saath rahenge

 1

 Consuming nut daily is very important to stay healthy
 akhrot main omega-3 fatty acid or fibre bharpoor maatra main paae jate hai
 a new study report has revealed that the consumption of walnuts reduces the risk of heart disease, stroke and diabetes
 study kii report main bataaya gaya he ki akhrot ke seven se sharir main good cholesterol kii maatra bad jaati he, jisase metabolic syndrome se peedit logon main tip-2 diabetes, dil kii beemaari or stroke kaa khatra kam hota he
 The study has been published in the journal Nutrition Research and Practice
 study ke liye shodhakartaaon ne metabolic syndrome se peedit 119 korean purush or mahilaon ko 2 group main baanta
 In this, a group was asked to consume 45 grams of walnuts per day for 16 weeks
 jabaki, duusare group ne white bread kaa seven kiya
 Both groups were asked to rest for 6 weeks at the end of 16 weeks
 iske baad donon grupon ko dobaaraa se 16 hafton ke liye akhrot or white bread die gaye
 During the test, lipid profile, HB1AC level, adiponectin levels as well as leptin, apolipoprotein b were measured four times with anthropometric and bioimpedance data
 metabolic syndrome se hone vaali 5 gambhir bimaariyaan jaise- blad sugar, blaj pressure, cholesterol level, triglisride or pet kaa fat bhi mapa gaya
 The results showed that the consumption of walnuts significantly improved the health of people suffering from metabolic syndrome

 electranik korporation of india (isiaiel) ke ejeeniyar bhi gananaa kendron par upasthit hai, taaki kisi tarah kii takneekee dikkat hone par ve turant use thik kar saken
 78 companies of Central Security Forces have been deployed for the security of polling machines
 pashchim bengal main is baar kaa vidhansabha chunaav is myne main khaas he ki bhartiya janata party bhi puure damaum ke saath maidan main utari he or isliye siyaasi ladaai or dilachasp ho gai he
 The West Bengal ruling Trinamool Congress is contesting on its own and has fielded candidates for all seats
 vahiin vammorcha evam congress ke bich gathbandhan he jahaan vammorcha mote taur par 200 siton par or congress kareeb 80 siton par chunaav lard rahi he
 For the first time in the election, 9776 voters got the right to exercise their franchise who became citizens of India after the exchange of territory between India and Bangladesh
 rajya main chunaav prachaar kii kaman trinmul congress kii ore se jahaan mukhyamantri mamata banerjee ne sanbhali, vahiin congress kii ore se sthaneey netaaon ke alaava congress adhyaksh sonia gandhi, upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi ne or vammorcha se buddhadev dasgupta, vimaan bose, seetaram yechuri samet kai diggajon ne prachaar kiya
 Many leaders including Prime Minister Narendra Modi, BJP President Amit Shah, Home Minister Rajnath Singh campaigned on behalf of the BJP
 trinmul congress ko sharada ghotaale or apane kuch netaaon ke kathith naarad sting main funsane jaise mudde se rubaru hona padaa
 The Trinamool's rival parties made it a point of campaigning
 kolkata shahar main bichombich ek fliover kaa gir janaa bhi chunavi mudda rahaa
 However, the Trinamool Congress introduced programs such as road construction in rural areas, good availability of electricity, cycles for girl students and one kg rice for two rupees
 vammorcha-congress ne talmail karke sattarudh trinmul ke saamne chunauti pesh kii or anek muddon par mamata banerjee kii party ko gheraa
 The Trinamool Congress has 184 seats in the current assembly of West Bengal
 congress 42 vidhayakon ke saath duusare sthaan par he jabaki marxvaadi communist party ke paas 40 vidhayak hai
 However, according to the exit poll, there is no change of power in West Bengal
 mamata banerjee satta main bani rahengi
 ABP Anand has predicted 178 seats for the ruling Trinamool Congress
 pichley vidhansabha chunaav main trinmul ko 184 siten mili thim
 The left-congress alliance is predicted to get 110 seats
 vampanthi partiyon or congress ko pichley chunaav main kul 103 siten mili thim, lekin pichley chunaav main trinmul congress or congress kaa gathbandhan tha
 India today-axis My India predicted Trinamool to get 233-253 seats in the 294-member West Bengal assembly, while the left-congress alliance predicted only 38 to 51 seats
 bhaajapa evam anya ko 5-5 siten milane kii sambhaavna he
 The comments times nau-si voter ne trinmul congress ko 167, vampanthi partiyon ko 75 or congress ko 45 siten milane kii sambhaavna jataai he
 It expected the BJP to get 4 and three other seats
 todes chanakya ne trinmul ko 210 jabaki vam-congress gathbandhan ko 70 or bhaajapa ko 14 siten milane kaa purvanumaan kiya he
 It is expected that by 12 noon a clear picture of the winners will be revealed and it will be clear whether Mamata didi remains in West Bengal or the Left Front has managed to regain its old status, which has an alliance with the Congress
 294-sadasyeey pashchim bengal vidhansabha ke prayek kshetra ke liye ek-ek gananaa prekshak niyukt kiya gaya he
 Engineers of the Electronic Corporation of India (ECIL) are also present at the counting centers, so that they can immediately correct any technical problem
 kendriya suraksha balon kii 78 companiyaan matdaan mashiinon kii suraksha main tainaat kii gai hai

 pashchim bengal sattarudh trinmul congress akele dam par chunaav lard rahi he or usne sabhi siton par ummidavaar utaare hai

 trinmul ke pratidwandvi dalon ne ise prachaar kaa mudda banaaya

 himachal pradesh ke kullu jile se ek iesai agent ke giraftaar hone kaa maamla saamne aayaa he
 The arrested agent was living in Kullu for the last 5 months
 agent ke do saathi isse pehle iesai se sambandh hone ke aarope main dilli main giraftaar ho chuke hai
 The ISI agent is named Avid Khan (25 years)
 aavid khan kullu jile ke banjaar sthit welieverj carch sidhvaan ilaake main rah rahaa tha
 Police have seized mobile, laptop and passport etc
 items found from Avid
 police ke mutabik, aaropee aavid kuch hi dinon main yahaan se indonesia jane vaala tha
 According to the police, the girl in Indonesia is an avid girl
 vahaan pahunchane ke baad aavid syria ravaanaa hone vaala tha
 The accused agent has also once gone to Sri Lanka from Kullu
 kullu jile ke espi ne bataaya ki aaropee yahaan paul (nakli naam) naam se rah rahaa tha
 The agent's real name was revealed by his passport
 espi ne aage kaha, passport ke anusaar aaropee agent mul rup se bangaleru kaa rahane vaala he
 At present, the police has registered a case against the ISI agent under various sections of the IPC
 somvaar ko aaropee ko court main pesh kiya jayega, jahaan police aaropee kii remand kii maang karegi taaki usase poochtacha kii ja sake
 After the martyrdom of four soldiers in Pakistan's firing in Poonch in Jammu and Kashmir, the voice of the retort is getting louder
 sarkaar or sena ne ection kii baat kahi bhi he
 But the Vishwa Hindu Parishad has gone a step ahead of the answer and demanded war
 vihip ke antarrashtriya adhyaksh praveen togadiya ne kaha he ki bharat shoorveeron kaa desh he
 He said, 'our Army, Airforce, Navy, CISF, BSF, Police, Home Guards are all engaged in the security of the country day and night and are giving their martyrdom every day
 togadiya ne kaha ki pakistan lagaataar bharat par hamale kar rahaa he, har din jawan mar rahe hai
 In such a situation, the time to embrace Pakistan is over now
 sargical strike nahin, sidhaa yudhrajnneetik dalon ke alaava kai morchon se ek baar phir pakistan ke khilaaf sargical strike kii maang uth rahi hai
 But Togadia has gone ahead and appealed to the government for action
 togadiya ne kaha he ki ab sargical strike nahin, sarkaar pakistan se sidhaa yuddh kare
 Togadia also said, 'many families have lost their relatives in gaining independence and in border defense
 desh veergati praapt javaanon ko nahin bhuulegaa
 Nobody wants war, but Pakistan is constantly attacking India
 har din jawan mar rahe hai
 Enough to embrace Pakistanis
 kootneeti ke naam par kitni bali?sargical nahin, ab sidhaa yuddh
 Further, Togadia also said that patriotism and national defense are not just about raising slogans, giving speeches, hoisting flags
 ab sarkaar pakistan se yuddh kare, puraa desh uske saath khadaa rahegaa
 His elder son Tej Pratap Yadav, who is going to meet RJD president Lalu Prasad Yadav on his way to Ranchi, deteriorated in his health
 iske baad jahanabad main rukkar unhone apana chekup karaayaa
 The doctor examined and told that due to depression, blood pressure (BP) has reduced
 bataa den ki lalu se milane ke liye tejpratap yadav somvaar ko ranchi ravaanaa hue the
 Lalu Prasad Yadav is undergoing treatment at the Rims of Ranchi, but his sudden health deteriorated on the way
 iske baad tej pratap ne jahanabad main rukkar doctor ko dikhaaya
 Before leaving for Ranchi on Monday, Tej Pratap Yadav said that he was not interested in contesting the Lok Sabha elections and did not want to contest in 2019
 chhapra loksabhaa seat lalu parivaar kii paramparaagat seat rahi he
 However, when Lalu Prasad Yadav was convicted in the fodder scam, when Rabri Devi contested the last election from Chapra, she lost from there
 darasal loksabhaa chunaav najadik aate hi ab is baat ko lekar lagaataar kayaas lagaae ja rahe hai ki chhapra se chunaav koun ladega
 When Aishwarya Rai was married to Tej Pratap Yadav, her name also rose for this seat, but one, she was not yet 25 years old, and now there is no scope left after the divorce case is moved in court
 kayaas is baat ke bhi the ki lalu yadav ke samadhi or chandrika raay bhi chhapra se chunaav ladane ke icchhuk the
 It is believed that there was a reason for the rift between Tej Pratap and Aishwarya
 baharhaal tejpratap yadav ne ravivaar ko achaanak argedy daftaar ja kar phir se raajnneeti main sakriy hone kaa elaan kar diya
 On Monday, he left for Ranchi to meet his father on the same issue

 raashtrapati ne kaha ki bharat main aarthik pragati main teji laane ke liye kathin faisle lene kii jarurat he

 yah pichley ek dashak kii ausat salaana vikaas dar lagbhag aath fisadi kaaphi kam he
 "he said that the rate of economic boom has come down in the last two years due to domestic and global reasons

 " unhone sansad ke sanyukt satr ko pehali baar sambodhit karte hue kaha, "mahangaai dar dhire-dhire kam ho rahi he, lekin yah ab bhi ek samasya bani hui he

 aisi sthiti main aap liquid fund main nivesh karke seaving bank se doguna phayda kama sakate hai
 What is a liquid fund? a short-term investment fund is called a liquid fund
 ise mani market fund bhi kaha jaataa he
 Liquid funds are a better investment option to generate higher returns over a short period of time
 haalanki is fund main bhi kisi anya mutual kii tarah hi kuch risk bhi maujuud he
 But the most important thing about this fund is that here you can invest for any period ranging from 1 day to 1 year
 is fund main nivesh kaa sabase behatar phayda aapako prati maah apni bachi hui selary ke nivesh par mil saktaa he
 No penalty on exit
 You do not have to pay any kind of exit load when you withdraw your money from the liquid fund at any time
 vahiin kisi duusare mutual fund main aap shaamil hote hai yaa apana nivesh baahar nikaalte hai to aapako shulk adaa karnaa padataa he jise lod kehete hai
 Return on Investment can be up to 8%
 Financial experts believe that investing in different liquid funds can yield up to 8%
 vahiin kisi bhi bank ke seaving acount main sirf 4 fisadi kaa hi ritern mil paata he
 Whenever inflation rises in the country, the biggest danger remains that the central bank should pay interest on savings, which reduces your savings
 mahangaai ke dauraan bhi liquid fund aapako behatar ritern dene kaa vaada karata he
 You will get back in 24 hours
 One of the biggest advantages of your money fund is that you can get back your invested money by selling it in just 24 hours

 mahaj khabar ke aadhaar par kisi bhi fund main nivesh na karen

 Maharashtra and Goa Bar Council Vice President Ashish P
 deshmukh ne kaha ki hadtaal ko acchhee safalataa mil rahi he
 In our world, there is an abundance of people working with the right hand
 yahaan tak ki rhite ko sahi or left ko galat ke arth main bhi liya jaataa he
 Since childhood, we are taught that we should eat with right hand, try to write with that hand too
 left hand kaa istemaal karne waalon kaa sankhya bhi apekshaakrit kam he
 90 percent of the world's people write with the right hand
 duniya ke keval 10 fisadi log lefti hai
 This does not necessarily mean that left hand users are inferior in any way
 haalanki aisi aam manyata he ki left hand se kaam karne vaale asaamaanya or kamjor hote he
 Perhaps this is the reason why parents use the left hand many times, and sometimes they are also strict
 is baat kaa doosraa pahalu bhi he
 In the meantime, some such research and fact have come in front of us which completely demolish the old concepts
 ye research is baat kii taakid karti hai ki left hand kaa istemaal karne vaale log zyada pratibhavan hote hai
 Many veterans are also included in this list
 jaise- mahatma gandhi, baraak obama, amitabh bachchan, bill gates, ratan tata, saurabh ganguli, sachin tendulkar, nichol kidman, angelina jolly, karan johar
 But are you aware that these left-wing celebrities also have to face many problems many times
 to aaie jaanate he left hand se judi kuch khoobiyon or samasyaon ke bare main
 
 
 From cricket to all other sports, being a leftist has its advantages
 left hand kaa istemaal karne vaale log boxing, tennis jaise khelon main zyada achche hote hai
 Now look at the Marine who won the gold medal at the Rio Olympics 2016 by defeating Sindhu
 left handed logon kaa aikyuu level adhik hota he
 According to a study by New York's St
 Lawrence University, left-handed people have an IQ level higher than 140 for right-handed people
 left hand se kaam karne vaale log samvedansheel hote hai
 People who always use the left hand have a great speed in their hands
 lefti shaks rity shaks kii tulana main stroke jaisi samasya se jaldi ubarne kii kshamta rakhte hai
 They can listen to fast changing sounds more easily
 lefti paisa kamaane or kharch karne ke maamle main bhi rhite hadend logon se aage rahete hai
 It is not that everything in the left-handed world is good
 ve rosemara kii jindagi main kai samasyaon se bhi rubaru hote hai
 After all, what are their problems? 
 
 skool main bani bench-cheiron par likhnaa mushkil hota he kyonki yerite handdlogon ke hisaab se banaaye gayi hote he
 Writing on spiral bound copies is very difficult
 kanchi chalaanaa mushkil bharaa hota he
 Usually, the mouse of the computer in the office is on the right side only and left-handed people have to do it according to their left side each time
 left hedend logon ke liye guitar bajaanaa aasaan nahin hota
 Left-handed people tend to think before joining hands with any other person and many times they habitually push the left hand forward
 shortand jaise lipiyon ko likhane main pareshaani hoti he
 Typing on a touchscreen mobile or ipad is not easy
 tin openar istemaal karnaa bhi mushkil lagata he
 Credit cards and swipe machines are not designed keeping in mind the left-handed people
 ink pen se likhnaa mushkil hota he
 The problem of hitting the hand with the next person while giving exams or writing while sitting together is also common
 logon dwaara hameshaa aashcharya se poochna ki are tum lefti ho, aapako alag sa mahasoos karwaata he
 The problem of hitting the hand next to someone while sitting side-by-side with someone bothers you and the fellow
 edlt filmon kii sansani sani leyoni ne bharat main apane kadam kya rakhe, unki lokapriyata main koi kami aane kaa naam hi nahin le rahi he
 While she is doing Ragini MMS-2 with producers like Ekta Kapoor, she also has many endorsement deals
 yahi nahin, unhone item sang kii daud main bollywood kii badi heroinon ko karaari shikast de di he
 We are talking about producer Ekta Kapoor and director Sanjay Gupta's next film Shoot Out at Wadala
 film main bollywood kii superstar priyanka chopra ne pehali baar item number bubbly badmaash kiya he
 Not only this, Sunny Leone will also have an item number Laila Teri Le Legi in this film
 khaas baat yah he ki item sang main unki bhi yah pehali pari he
 But in the race for popularity, Sunny has defeated Priyanka
 utyub kii baat karen to priyanka ke item number ko relies hue teen hafte guzar chuke hai lekin use dekhne waalon kaa aankada lagbhag paanch lakh par hi pahunchaa he lekin laila ne pichley chah din main lagbhag paune nau lakh kaa aankada chhu liya he
 Of course Sunny is to be called after the porn star, but it is certain that her popularity figures in India are touching new heights every day
 uttar pradesh kii rajdhani lakhanu main aipal ke manageravivek tiwarihatyakand main giraftaar sipahiprashanth choudharike samarthan main utar rahe sipaahiyon se nipatane ke liye sarkaar orupi polisake afasar nai kavayad kar rahe hai
 The soldiers decided to protest after tying the black ribbon to protest
 haalanki, abhi tak is virodh ke hone kii koi khabar nahin he
 Immediately after the protest by the soldiers, the state government gave promotion to more than 25 thousand constables
 rajya main 25,091 consteble ko pramotion dekar head consteble bana diya gaya he
 It is believed that this step has been taken to allay the displeasure of the soldiers
 upi police ke consteble lambey samay se yah maang kar rahe the
 Apart from this, refresher and training session is being started by UP Police for constables posted in Lucknow zone
 isamen kareeb 6 hajaar consteble ko logon se samvaad behatar karne ke liye soft skill training di ja rahi he
 This exercise has also been done to stop the dissatisfaction with the action taken on the Vivek Tiwari murder case and the constable Prashant Chaudhary
 isse pehle, upi police ke sheersh afasaron ne virodh jataa rahe sipaahiyon par ection lekar bhi unhen sandesh dene kii koshish kii thi
 Two days ago, two constables - Keshav Dutt Pandey and Mohammed Shadab - who protested in the case, were suspended and 11 policemen were attached to the police line
 inamen ek sab-inspector bhi shaamil tha
 He protested against the action taken by constable Prashant Chaudhary by wearing a black ribbon
 vahiin, beete shuukravaar ko lakhanu main teen or eta main consteble ko suspend kiya gaya tha
 Two suspended policemen were also arrested from Varanasi and Mirzapur
 inhone kaala riban baandhne ke alaava hatyaropee pulisavaalon ke samarthan main abhiyaan bhi chalaaya gaya tha
 After protesting the soldiers by tying the Kali belt, there was a news that there is now a conspiracy among the UP police to not work anymore
 is sambandh main watsap massej forward kiye ja rahe the
 Who is sending this message to whom, it is not clear
 lekin is massej ke bare main meerut ke espi intelegence aar
 P
 pandey ne 9 jilon ke police vibhaag ko chitthee bheji thi
 However, DGP assured that he has full faith in his jawans
 unka bharosa sahi sabit hota dikh rahaa he
 The Confederation of All India Traders (CAIT) has raised serious concerns about goods being imported from China
 CAIT ne kaha ki isamen badi maatra main hawala kaarobaar kii ashanka he, jiske kaaran chini saamaan bazaar main sasta miltaa he or sarkaar ko custom duty va tex kii badi chapat lagati he
 CAIT also raised the question whether this money from hawala is given to Pakistan to carry out terrorist activities? Seeing the seriousness of the subject, CAIT has demanded from the government that all aspects of the case be investigated in depth and the culprits should be apprehended
 isamen kahin na kahin bhartiya bandargah ke adhikariyon kii mileebhagat he
 CAIT said that goods imported from China are billed for less than the cost and accordingly they are levied on duty and IGST
 isse sarkaar ko rajasav kii badi haani hoti he
 CAIT national president BC Bhartia and national general secretary Praveen Khandelwal said, 'most of the goods imported from China in our country come at very low price billing
 kai maamalon main to saamaan kuch aata he or uskaa bill kuch or hota he, jisase us par kam se kam duty or ijiesasti lagata he
 He said that if the goods coming through imports and the goods written in the bill are matched, then you will know how much difference there is between the two
 is baat ko dhyaan main rakhte hue bhartiya bandargahon par china se aane vaale saamaan par behad kadi nigaraanee kii aavashyaktaa he
 Bhartia and Khandelwal also said that in this case there is connivance with officials of various departments along with the importer, due to which the business has been running for a long time very easily
 isse na sirf bhartiya bazaar kaa maahaul kharaab ho rahaa he, balki desh kii suraksha ke liye sankat paidaa ho gaya he
 He also said that those who ask for goods from China and give IGST on it, should take IGST input credit as per the law, but if the matter is investigated, it will be found that no one has claimed input credit
 Is, because all those goods are sold in the market without bills and due to this these goods become cheaper
 vahiin, gharelu utpaada puraa tex dete hai, jisaki vajah se chini maal se mahange rahete he
 He said that this matter is also related to the security of the country
